     geoentity_1.owner AS owner_39,
     geoentity_1.id AS id,

     geoentity_1.activated AS activated_44,

     geoentity_1.siteMaster AS siteMaster_48,
     geoentity_1.lockedBy AS lockedBy_49,

     geoentity_1.seq AS seq_52,

FROM geoentity geoentity_1 
WHERE geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT country.id FROM country)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT province.id FROM province)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT district.id FROM district)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT adminpost.id FROM adminpost)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT locality.id FROM locality)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT city.id FROM city)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT town.id FROM town)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT village.id FROM village)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT abstractsite.id FROM abstractsite)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT facility.id FROM facility)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT trap.id FROM trap)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT sprayzone.id FROM sprayzone)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT permanentwaterbody.id FROM permanentwaterbody)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT river.id FROM river)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT road.id FROM road)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT nationalroad.id FROM nationalroad)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT reserve.id FROM reserve)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT railway.id FROM railway)
ORDER BY  id ASC

WHERE geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT country.id FROM country)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT province.id FROM province)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT district.id FROM district)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT adminpost.id FROM adminpost)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT locality.id FROM locality)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT city.id FROM city)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT town.id FROM town)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT village.id FROM village)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT abstractsite.id FROM abstractsite)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT facility.id FROM facility)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT trap.id FROM trap)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT sprayzone.id FROM sprayzone)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT permanentwaterbody.id FROM permanentwaterbody)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT river.id FROM river)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT road.id FROM road)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT nationalroad.id FROM nationalroad)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT reserve.id FROM reserve)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT railway.id FROM railway)
ORDER BY  id ASC

WHERE geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT country.id FROM country)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT province.id FROM province)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT district.id FROM district)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT adminpost.id FROM adminpost)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT locality.id FROM locality)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT city.id FROM city)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT town.id FROM town)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT village.id FROM village)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT abstractsite.id FROM abstractsite)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT facility.id FROM facility)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT trap.id FROM trap)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT sprayzone.id FROM sprayzone)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT permanentwaterbody.id FROM permanentwaterbody)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT river.id FROM river)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT road.id FROM road)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT nationalroad.id FROM nationalroad)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT reserve.id FROM reserve)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT railway.id FROM railway)
ORDER BY  id ASC

     GeometryFromText(NULL) AS lineString_30,
     GeometryFromText(NULL) AS lineString_32,
     GeometryFromText(NULL) AS lineString_34,
     GeometryFromText(NULL) AS polygon_36,
     GeometryFromText(NULL) AS lineString_38,
     geoentity_1.owner AS owner_39,
     geoentity_1.id AS id,
     geoentity_1.gazId AS gazId_40,
     geoentity_1.entityName AS entityName_41,
     geoentity_1.createDate AS createDate_42,
     geoentity_1.keyName AS keyName_43,
     geoentity_1.activated AS activated_44,
     geoentity_1.lastUpdateDate AS lastUpdateDate_45,
     geoentity_1.type AS type_46,
     geoentity_1.lastUpdatedBy AS lastUpdatedBy_47,
     geoentity_1.siteMaster AS siteMaster_48,
     geoentity_1.lockedBy AS lockedBy_49,
     geoentity_1.entityDomain AS entityDomain_50,
     geoentity_1.createdBy AS createdBy_51,
     geoentity_1.seq AS seq_52,
     geoentity_1.geoId AS geoId_53,
     geoentity_1.id AS id
FROM geoentity geoentity_1 
WHERE geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT country.id FROM country)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT province.id FROM province)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT district.id FROM district)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT adminpost.id FROM adminpost)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT locality.id FROM locality)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT city.id FROM city)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT town.id FROM town)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT village.id FROM village)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT abstractsite.id FROM abstractsite)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT facility.id FROM facility)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT trap.id FROM trap)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT sprayzone.id FROM sprayzone)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT permanentwaterbody.id FROM permanentwaterbody)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT river.id FROM river)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT road.id FROM road)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT nationalroad.id FROM nationalroad)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT reserve.id FROM reserve)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT railway.id FROM railway)
ORDER BY  id ASC 

LIMIT 20 OFFSET 0

     GeometryFromText(NULL) AS lineString_38,
     geoentity_1.owner AS owner_39,
     geoentity_1.id AS id,
     geoentity_1.gazId AS gazId_40,
     geoentity_1.entityName AS entityName_41,
     geoentity_1.createDate AS createDate_42,
     geoentity_1.keyName AS keyName_43,
     geoentity_1.activated AS activated_44,
     geoentity_1.lastUpdateDate AS lastUpdateDate_45,
     geoentity_1.type AS type_46,
     geoentity_1.lastUpdatedBy AS lastUpdatedBy_47,
     geoentity_1.siteMaster AS siteMaster_48,
     geoentity_1.lockedBy AS lockedBy_49,
     geoentity_1.entityDomain AS entityDomain_50,
     geoentity_1.createdBy AS createdBy_51,
     geoentity_1.seq AS seq_52,
     geoentity_1.geoId AS geoId_53,
     geoentity_1.id AS id
FROM geoentity geoentity_1 
WHERE geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT country.id FROM country)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT province.id FROM province)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT district.id FROM district)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT adminpost.id FROM adminpost)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT locality.id FROM locality)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT city.id FROM city)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT town.id FROM town)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT village.id FROM village)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT abstractsite.id FROM abstractsite)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT facility.id FROM facility)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT trap.id FROM trap)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT sprayzone.id FROM sprayzone)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT permanentwaterbody.id FROM permanentwaterbody)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT river.id FROM river)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT road.id FROM road)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT nationalroad.id FROM nationalroad)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT reserve.id FROM reserve)
AND geoentity_1.id NOT IN (SELECT railway.id FROM railway)
ORDER BY  id ASC
